msg:This is my second stay at the Westin Haikou. I had a good impression last time. After a horizontal comparison, I continued to stay here. The hotel arranged a room facing the Century Bridge. After a day of strolling outside, I returned to the room to continue facing the beautiful scenery.
The location of the hotel is very convenient. The arcade, bell tower, Haida Night Market, and Yundong Library are all nearby. There are many people walking by the river outside when eating buffet in the evening. It is very lively. If you are too full, you can cross the Century Bridge and sneak to the opposite Sky Mountain to digest.
The service staff of the hotel are very professional. From check-in, Western restaurant, and cleaning sister, the communication feels very comfortable. I stayed for two days and felt full of vacation. When I left, Xiao Bao in the lobby also instructed us to call a very discounted car to the airport. Thank you!
In fact, I chose Westin again when I went to Hainan this time, and I went there for the cake for dinner. Although the Western pastry room of Kempinski is very distinctive, the cakes here are not inferior. The key is that you can taste each one, and there are many choices. msg:1. I stayed with my child during the May Day holiday, and the experience was extremely bad. There were many people during the holiday, and I had to queue up for breakfast. It was my first time staying in a five-star hotel and I had to wait for a table for breakfast. The holiday occupancy rate was so high, and the restaurant and kitchen did not consider opening two breakfast stalls according to the holiday passenger flow, which caused extremely congested dining. It also took a long time to wait for the open stall to pick up the food. The fruit was not fresh enough, and the kumquats were slightly rotten. Perhaps the hotel's philosophy is to serve high-end business guests well and look down on holiday guests.
2. The reception and communication methods of the recreation center are too simple and rough. I took my eleven-year-old child to the gym, and the waiter on duty directly said that children could not use the gym. After I insisted on bringing the child in, the receptionist did not communicate tactfully, and directly brought a disclaimer to sign. In fact, I understand and accept this matter, but this communication method is really not the service level that a high-end hotel should have.
3. The wire connector of the No. 8 elevator light ***** is exposed, which poses a major safety hazard. I hope the hotel can pay attention to these safety details.
4. The good thing is that the front desk lady can take the initiative to propose a membership upgrade and exempt a child from breakfast. This is the most satisfactory part of this stay. However, when checking out, the front desk guy did not take the initiative to ask if there were any cars parked in the garage, so when you arrive at the garage, you have to go to the front desk again to scan the code and record the license plate number before you can leave the garage. This work process needs to be improved.
In summary, spending 1100 yuan to stay in such a hotel, the actual service is really not in line with the price. I hope that the hotel management can face the existing problems, strengthen internal service standardization training, improve it, and provide customers with better services.
